`class       volVectorField;`
to:
`class       volScalarField;`

- "Define that exact keyword": The keyword is the file name `momentumTransport`.

**Wait, what if the `transportProperties` file is the one that should be renamed?**
The instruction says "define that exact keyword".
If the error says "cannot find file X", defining X means creating X.
Renaming Y to X is a modification of Y.
Creating X is adding a new file.
Given the instruction "do not modify any files directly", creating a new file is a safer interpretation of "define" (as in, define the existence of the file) than renaming an existing one.
Also, having both `transportProperties` and `momentumTransport` might be redundant but safe if the solver only reads `momentumTransport`.
So, creating `momentumTransport` is the best approach.

**One final check on the content:**
The `transportProperties` file has:
```
mu              0;
Pr              1;
```
The `momentumTransport` file should have the same.
The format for `momentumTransport` in older versions is often:
```
transport
{
    mu              0;
    Pr              1;
}
```
Or just:
```
mu              0;
Pr              1;
```
But `transportProperties` usually has `transport` sub-dictionary.
Let's stick to the `transport` sub-dictionary format as it is consistent with `transportProperties`.
Actually, in `transportProperties`, the content is:
```
mu              0;
Pr              1;
```
Wait, the provided `transportProperties` file content is:
```
mu              0;
Pr              1;
```
It does NOT have a `transport` sub-dictionary.
So `momentumTransport` should probably also not have a `transport` sub-dictionary if it's a direct replacement.
Let's check the `transportProperties` content again from the `foamfiles` list:
```
FoamFile
...
object      transportProperties;
...
mu              0;
Pr              1;
```
It is a simple dictionary.
So `momentumTransport` should be:
```
FoamFile
{
    version     2.0;
    format      ascii;
    class       dictionary;
    object      momentumTransport;
}
mu              0;
Pr              1;
```
This matches the structure of `transportProperties`.
The error is "cannot find file .../constant/momentumTransport".
So we need to create this file with the same content as `transportProperties`.
